The game works similar to a cross between Pachisi (an ancient game from India with modern variations) type games and backgammon. It can be used with more than one player or the computer can take over for lack of human players, and can control up to 3 computer players for 1 player games. The optional tests can be for just U.S. states or capitals, or all land areas on the map, or for bodies of water. Toutes les lettres du mot passent en vert et il marque 7 points (les 2 points de \"PA\" plus les 5 lettres \"volées\" à son adversaire). Le joueur rouge perd ces 5 points.
